Date: 2022-08-02 05:09:43
Caption: Hexagonia tenuis fungi is plentiful in the regenerating native forests at the base of the escarpment. These areas were originally cleared for farmland and mining. The returning forests are only approximately 50 years into the process of establishing themselves again and I'm always in awe of their regenerative power. It's hard not to amorphosize natural phenomena with the constraints our language puts upon us. Fungi networks are described like the internet, beehives are described like officeworkers, but we know this is a crude way to narrate the complexity, abstraction, mystery and full expression of nature. So I tread tentatively knowing these words that follow are inept, but to experience a regenerating forest is to be part of a continual homecoming. With each species of native flora and fauna that returns I personally am exalted but there is no fanfare, fireworks or roll call within the forest itself. Instead a palatable gathering of strength and an emerging tranquillity spreads as each species reestablishes itself within the dynamics of the forest family. Many of the photos in this gallery are from this regenerating forest and it is a joy to share the homecoming of species like this fungi with you. #mycology #mycologysociety #fungus #mycologyphotography #fungilover #fungiphotography #fungifanatic #fantasticfungi #fungiofinstagram #fungiownunder #fungihunter #fungiaustralia #fungifreaks #fungihunting #fungiidentification #fungikingdom #fungilove #fungiphotography #fungioftheday #mushroom #mushrooms #mushlove #mushroomphotography #mushroomsofinstagram #australianfungi #fungi #forestbathing #forestfinds #naturesbeauty #forestlovers #biodiversity

Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Now we can legally grow this, I was curious to give it a go - especially after investing so much time into trying to grow Cordyceps gunnii, unsuccessfully! Not my best grow! And I have been watching lots of US growers really get to dial these in to be an art. But I grew these on white rice with no nutrients to start out so I could get an idea of growth, yield, and other characteristics that may help later! One big hint, don't try to grow these when it is hot without cooling! #guerrillamycology #fungiculture #ğŸ„ #fungi #fungus #funghi #hongos #myceliumrunning #radicalmycology #radmycology #thinkfungi #mycology #mycophile #mycophilia #mycelium #mushrooms #myceliumrunning #myceliumnetwork #myceliummood #cordyceps #cordycepsmilitaris #cordycepsgunnii #introducedfungi #notnativefungi #notwildfungi #ethnomycology #entheogenicfungi #fungiphotography #mushroomphotography

Caption: Growing a new fungus is always interesting. This is Cordyceps militaris #cordycepsmilitaris a fungi that until recently was not allowed to be grown here in Australia. Now we can legally grow this, I was curious to give it a go - especially after investing so much time into trying to grow Cordyceps gunnii, unsuccessfully! Not my best grow! And I have been watching lots of US growers really get to dial these in to be an art. But I grew these on white rice with no nutrients to start out so I could get an idea of growth, yield, and other characteristics that may help later! Fungus Polyporales Trunk Mushroom Medicinal mushroom Jungle Lingzhi mushroom Inonotus Agaricomycetes Hen-of-the-wood
Date: 2022-08-02 05:09:43
Caption: Hexagonia tenuis fungi is plentiful in the regenerating native forests at the base of the escarpment. These areas were originally cleared for farmland and mining. The returning forests are only approximately 50 years into the process of establishing themselves again and I'm always in awe of their regenerative power. It's hard not to amorphosize natural phenomena with the constraints our language puts upon us. Fungi networks are described like the internet, beehives are described like officeworkers, but we know this is a crude way to narrate the complexity, abstraction, mystery and full expression of nature. So I tread tentatively knowing these words that follow are inept, but to experience a regenerating forest is to be part of a continual homecoming. With each species of native flora and fauna that returns I personally am exalted but there is no fanfare, fireworks or roll call within the forest itself. Instead a palatable gathering of strength and an emerging tranquillity spreads as each species reestablishes itself within the dynamics of the forest family. Many of the photos in this gallery are from this regenerating forest and it is a joy to share the homecoming of species like this fungi with you. #mycology #mycologysociety #fungus #mycologyphotography #fungilover #fungiphotography #fungifanatic #fantasticfungi #fungiofinstagram #fungiownunder #fungihunter #fungiaustralia #fungifreaks #fungihunting #fungiidentification #fungikingdom #fungilove #fungiphotography #fungioftheday #mushroom #mushrooms #mushlove #mushroomphotography #mushroomsofinstagram #australianfungi #fungi #forestbathing #forestfinds #naturesbeauty #forestlovers #biodiversity
